[30;1m2 | [0m[35m Usage[0m
[30;1m3 | [0m[35m=======[0m
[30;1m4 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m5 | [0m[35mEvery long running service process should have a call to install a[0m
[30;1m6 | [0m[35msignal handler which will trigger the guru meditation framework upon[0m
